posted:Posted December 26, 2023
msg:Hilton Garden Inn is a good value for money hotel. The price is not much more expensive than Hilton Garden Inn in the same city, so it is more cost-effective!

The room is really big and warm. In the rare cold wave that makes the lowest temperature in Heyuan, which has no winter, reach freezing point in the early morning, the room is the most comfortable without turning on the heater!

Hardware missing: For a hotel of Hilton Garden Inn's level, it is really disqualified to not have a washlet on the toilet!

Breakfast: After staying in the Hakka area (Nanjing, Meixian, and Meizhou, Zhangzhou, Fujian) for many days, this morning is the first meal for human beings! A wide variety of breads, delicious pork sausages and bacon, sunny-side-up eggs and omelettes made for guests, salads and lettuce that can be eaten raw, and freshly ground coffee from a fully automatic coffee machine. This is the breakfast of humans or Homo sapiens! No more eating those Hakka B&Bs (the key is that they are not cheap and more expensive than Hilton) with only boiled eggs, steamed buns, white porridge, steamed dumplings, peanut soy milk, and even fried eggs and ham slices/bacon/sausages. Neanderthal "breakfast"!

Parking: There is a hotel area in the basement, scan the code before leaving.

Ctrip 6-choose-2 gift: I chose milk and fruit.

100 yuan voucher for Chinese restaurant: This is very practical. I can order what I want to eat at the Chinese restaurant with peace of mind and only spent 170 yuan in the end.
